### [39] [PACE: A Neuro-Symbolic Framework for Plausible and Actionable Counterfactual Explanations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01306)
*Pavel Iakovets,Liyanapathiranage Sudeepika Wajirakumari Samarathunga,Martin Thomas Horsch,Fadi Al Machot*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: PACE 是一个模块化的神经符号框架，通过将神经网络预测与符号推理（ASP）分离，在生成反事实解释时强制执行领域约束，从而产生既有效又符合现实可行性的可操作解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有反事实解释方法虽能生成改变预测的替代方案，但因缺乏显式的领域知识和干预约束机制，常给出不现实或不可行的建议。亟需一种能结合数据驱动预测与符号推理的方法，确保解释兼具有效性与可行性。

Method: 提出 PACE 框架，将预测与推理解耦为两个组件：多层感知器（MLP）用于分类预测，回答集编程（ASP）规则用于编码领域约束（如教育、职业、工时的可行修改及不可变属性的保护），在反事实生成阶段由符号推理层强制执行约束。

Result: 在 Adult Income 数据集上的案例研究表明，符号约束能在反事实有效性与合理性之间取得平衡，生成的解释更好地满足领域特定的可行性要求。

Conclusion: 神经符号方法为可解释 AI 中透明且可行性感知的反事实解释提供了有前景的路径，PACE 具有模型无关性和领域适应性，适用于需要现实决策支持的应用场景。

Abstract: Counterfactual explanations explain machine learning predictions by identifying minimal input changes that would alter a model's decision. Although many existing methods successfully generate prediction-changing alternatives, they often produce unrealistic or infeasible recommendations due to a lack of explicit mechanisms for incorporating domain knowledge and intervention constraints. Neuro-symbolic AI offers a promising direction by combining data-driven predictive models with symbolic reasoning capable of representing human-understandable rules and feasible actions. This paper presents PACE, a modular neuro-symbolic framework for generating feasibility-aware counterfactual explanations. The framework separates prediction and reasoning into two components: a neural predictive model for classification and a symbolic reasoning layer that enforces domain-specific constraints during counterfactual generation. By explicitly modeling feasible interventions, the framework produces explanations consistent with domain knowledge while remaining interpretable and actionable. The approach is model-agnostic and adaptable to domains requiring realistic decision support. A case study is conducted on the Adult Income dataset, combining a multilayer perceptron classifier with Answer Set Programming (ASP) rules encoding feasible modifications to education, occupation, and working hours while preserving immutable attributes. Results highlight the trade-off between counterfactual validity and plausibility and show that symbolic constraints yield explanations that better satisfy domain-specific feasibility requirements, illustrating the potential of neuro-symbolic methods for transparent, feasibility-aware counterfactual explanation in explainable AI.

</details>


### [40] [Auto-FL-Research: Agentic Search for Federated Learning Algorithms](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01366)
*Holger R. Roth,Ziyue Xu,Chester Chen,Daguang Xu,Peter Cnudde,Andrew Feng*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出 Auto-FL-Research (AFR)，一个受约束的编码智能体工作流，用于自动搜索联邦学习算法配方（优化器、聚合规则、训练调度等），在多个医疗和 LEAF 基准上验证其有效性，同时揭示了种子敏感性、单次运行伪影等混合结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 联邦学习研究中存在大量小但关键的算法选择（优化器变体、服务器聚合规则、本地训练调度、归一化、正则化、模型架构等），手动探索成本高且难以公平比较，因为候选改动可能改变训练或评估路径。

Method: 提出 AFR，一个受约束的编码智能体工作流：智能体可提议并实现候选训练算法（含服务器聚合规则、客户端更新调度、本地目标函数和注册模型变体）；任务配置文件固定变异表面、计算预算、通信合约和最终模型评估；每个搜索活动记录候选分数、运行时间、编辑文件、产物及失败状态。

Result: 在 5 个医疗跨孤岛 FLamby 任务和 5 个固定 LEAF 数据集 + LEAF 合成任务的分组客户端配置上评估，5 种子重复实验在 4 个 FLamby 任务和 5/6 个 LEAF 配置上取得增益，同时暴露了种子敏感和搜索选择的失败案例。等预算对照实验表明部分增益来自 FL 配方改变，其他则来自固定表面的标量调优或单次运行伪影。

Conclusion: 混合结果是贡献的一部分：展示了如何将智能体生成的候选方案分解为可复现的 FL 机制、固定表面调优效应和被选择的单次运行伪影，为 FL 自动化算法搜索提供了系统化的分析框架。

Abstract: Federated learning (FL) research often depends on many small but consequential algorithmic choices: optimizer variants, server aggregation rules, local training schedules, normalization, regularization, and model architecture. These choices are expensive to explore manually and difficult to compare fairly when candidate changes can also alter the FL training or evaluation path. In this work, we present Auto-FL-Research (AFR), a constrained coding-agent workflow for FL algorithmic recipe search. Agents may propose and implement candidate training algorithms, including server aggregation rules, client update schedules, local objectives, and registered model variants, while task profiles fix the mutation surface, compute budget, communication contract, and final model evaluation. Each campaign records candidate scores, runtime, edited files, artifacts, and failure status. We evaluate AFR on five healthcare cross-silo FLamby tasks and on grouped-client profiles for the five fixed LEAF datasets plus the LEAF synthetic task. Five-seed repeat evaluations support gains on four FLamby tasks and five of six LEAF profiles, while also exposing seed-sensitive and search-selected failure cases. Same-budget controls show that several gains correspond to FL-recipe changes, whereas other improvements are recovered by fixed-surface scalar controls or fail under repeat or held-out evaluation. These mixed outcomes are part of the contribution: they show how agent-generated candidates can be separated into repeated FL mechanisms, fixed-surface tuning effects, and selected single-run artifacts.

</details>


### [41] [The Wiola Architecture for Efficient Small Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01394)
*Aryuemaan Kumar Chowdhury,Afreen Shaik,Yaparla Bhargavi,Brahma Kumar*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: Wiola 是一个完全原创的小型语言模型架构，引入了五项独立创新：螺旋旋转位置编码(SRPE)、门控跨层注意力(GCLA)、自适应Token合并(ATM)、双流前馈网络(DSFF)和带偏移向量的RMSNorm变体。该模型与现有模型家族无结构关联，发布了四种规模，并完全兼容HuggingFace生态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前主流语言模型（GPT、LLaMA、Mistral等）在架构上存在高度同质化，缺乏真正从第一性原理出发的原创设计。作者旨在构建一个与任何现有模型家族无结构渊源的SLM架构，通过多项独立创新来探索Transformer架构的改进空间。

Method: Wiola 集成了五项独立创新：(1) SRPE：在三维螺旋流形上嵌入位置信息，融合绝对、相对和层次位置信号；(2) GCLA：每个解码层通过软交叉注意力访问前两层压缩摘要，增强层间一致性；(3) ATM：在网络中间层动态合并语义冗余的相邻token，降低注意力复杂度；(4) DSFF：用两个并行的前馈流加可学习的逐维度门控融合，替代传统MLP；(5) WiolaRMSNorm：在RMSNorm基础上引入可学习的逐维度偏移向量，防止表征崩塌。模型提供完整的数学推导、架构框图、复杂度分析，发布四种规模（120M/360M/700M/1.5B参数），并通过22项架构单元测试。

Result: Wiola 发布了四种参数规模（120M、360M、700M、1.5B），所有22项架构单元测试均通过，完全兼容HuggingFace Transformers生态系统。

Conclusion: Wiola 证明了从第一性原理出发构建原创SLM架构的可行性。通过五项独立创新组件，该模型在保持与主流框架兼容的同时，提供了有别于现有模型家族的全新架构范式。

Abstract: We present Wiola, a fully original Small Language Model (SLM) architecture built from first principles, sharing no structural lineage with any existing model family including GPT, LLaMA, Mistral, or Falcon. Wiola introduces five independently novel components: (i) Spiral Rotary Positional Encoding (SRPE), which embeds token positions on a three-dimensional helical manifold combining absolute, relative, and hierarchical positional signals; (ii) Gated Cross-Layer Attention (GCLA), providing each decoder layer with soft cross-attention access to compressed summaries of two preceding layers for inter-layer coherence; (iii) Adaptive Token Merging (ATM), which dynamically merges se mantically redundant adjacent tokens in middle network layers to reduce attention complexity without information loss; (iv) Dual Stream Feed-Forward (DSFF), replacing the conventional MLP with two parallel streams fused by a learned per-dimension gate; and (v) WiolaRMSNorm, a modified normalisation introducing a per-dimension learned offset vector that prevents representation collapse. We provide complete mathematical derivations, architectural block diagrams, complexity analyses, and systematic comparisons against GPT-2, LLaMA-2, and Mistral. Wiola is released in four sizes (120M, 360M, 700M, and 1.5B parameters) and is fully compatible with the HuggingFace Transformers ecosystem, with all 22 architectural unit tests passing.

</details>


### [42] [Agent4cs: A Multi-agent System for Code Summarization in Large Hierarchical Codebases](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01425)
*Yongjian Tang,Ezgi Sarikayak,Doruk Tuncel,Jie M. Zhang,Thomas Runkler*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: Agent4cs 提出了一种自底向上的多智能体框架，通过摘要生成、关键词提取和质量保证三个专门化智能体协同工作，解决了大型代码仓库的结构化理解问题，在语义一致性和关键词覆盖率上显著优于基线方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有代码摘要方案通常依赖单一语言模型，将源代码视为扁平文本处理，忽视了代码仓库内部的丰富依赖关系和层次结构信息，尤其对混淆结构和文档不完整的代码库理解效果不佳。

Method: 提出 Agent4cs 多智能体框架，采用自底向上方式对大型代码库进行摘要。包含三个专门化智能体：摘要智能体负责生成鲁棒的代码摘要；关键词提取智能体主动从子文件夹中识别关键信息；质量保证智能体迭代优化输出的可读性、连贯性和完整性。

Result: 在 7 个前沿模型上评估，Agent4cs 在所有文件夹层级上的语义一致性相比两种结构化提示基线平均提升 8%；在真实世界数据集上，归一化关键词覆盖率提升高达 38%。

Conclusion: Agent4cs 通过多智能体协作和层次化处理策略，有效提升了大型代码仓库的自动化摘要质量，证明了利用代码结构信息和专门化智能体分工的优越性。

Abstract: Understanding large, complex codebases, especially those with obfuscated structures and incomplete documentation, remains a significant challenge. Existing code summarization solutions often rely on a single language model or coding assistant like Claude Code, and treat source code as flat text, underutilizing the rich interdependencies and hierarchical information within a repository. To address these shortcomings, we propose Agent4cs - a multi-agent framework that summarizes large codebases in a bottom-up fashion, where a summarization agent focuses on producing robust summaries; a keyword-extraction agent proactively identifies critical information from subfolders; and a quality-assurance agent iteratively refines the outputs for readability, coherence, and completeness. Evaluated on 7 frontier models, Agent4cs improves semantic consistency across all folder levels by average 8% compared to two structured prompting baselines with code segments. Furthermore, extensive evaluation on real-world datasets demonstrates up to 38% gains in normalized keyword coverage rate over the same baselines.

### [43] [When Should Service Agents Reconsider? Difficulty-Routed Control in Customer-Service Operations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01426)
*Qian Chen,Chengyuan Liu,Xin Yu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于难度路由的服务控制架构，通过轻量级路由器识别存在操作冲突的客服会话，并将其升级到包含冲突感知通信和写触发重审机制的增强工作流，从而在保持常规服务低摩擦的同时，将额外的深思熟虑和安全防护集中于可能产生后端写入错误的关键环节。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自主客服智能体正从对话交互转向操作执行（退款、取消、换货等），但这带来了服务控制问题：企业需要在保持服务效率的同时，防止在客户指令、策略约束、企业记录和后端写入相互交织的请求中出现操作错误。现有方案缺乏针对性，无法区分常规请求与高风险请求。

Method: 提出难度路由服务控制架构：(1) 轻量级路由器判断会话是否需要升级处理；(2) 常规会话保持在低成本基线路径上处理；(3) 操作耦合会话被路由到升级工作流，该工作流包含冲突感知通信（conflict-aware communication）和写触发重审（write-triggered reconsideration）机制，将额外的审慎检查和安全防护集中于后端写入前的关键阶段。

Result: 在τ²-bench的人工验证零售和航空任务上评估：(1) 零售场景中，方法在处理有操作冲突的服务请求时一致性提升；(2) 路由证据显示更强的控制被定向到冲突请求而非常规请求；(3) 对话和工具使用分析表明，性能提升并非来自无差别的交互扩展或更广泛的工具链，额外的轮次和工具调用主要用于证据收集、写入分离和写入前重审；(4) 升级工作流能够保留备选方案、将检索到的记录绑定到正确操作、序列化写入、分解多实体请求；(5) 航空场景的结果将相同的服务控制逻辑扩展到了预订操作。

Conclusion: 难度路由服务控制架构能有效解决操作耦合场景下的服务可靠性问题，通过将审慎控制集中于高风险写入环节，而非对所有会话施加统一控制，实现了效率与安全的平衡，且该逻辑可跨领域扩展。

Abstract: Autonomous customer-service agents are shifting from conversational interfaces toward operational execution roles: they retrieve firm records, apply service policies, and execute backend writes such as refunds, cancellations, exchanges, order modifications, and reservation changes. This shift creates a service-control problem: firms must keep routine service fast and low-friction while preventing operational errors on requests where customer instructions, policy constraints, firm records, and backend writes interact. We propose a difficulty-routed service-control architecture that asks when service agents should reconsider before acting. A lightweight router keeps routine sessions on a low-cost baseline path and routes operationally coupled sessions to an escalated workflow. The escalated path uses conflict-aware communication and write-triggered reconsideration to concentrate deliberation and safeguards before consequential backend writes, rather than applying additional control uniformly across all service sessions. We evaluate the architecture on human-verified retail and airline tasks from $τ^{2}$-bench. In retail, the method improves reliability consistently on service requests with operational conflict. Routing evidence shows that stronger control is directed toward conflicted requests rather than broadly applied to routine ones. Dialogue and tool-use profiles suggest that gains do not come from indiscriminate interaction expansion or broader tool chains; instead, added turns and tool calls support evidence gathering, write separation, and pre-write reconsideration. Case-level evidence shows that the escalated workflow preserves fallback plans, binds retrieved records to the correct action, sequences writes, and decomposes multi-entity requests. Airline results extend the same service-control logic to reservation operations.

</details>


### [44] [CreativityNeuro: Steering Language Model Weights to Improve Divergent Thinking and Reduce Mode Collapse](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01433)
*Samuel Schapiro,Core Francisco Park,Felix Sosa,Lav R. Varshney*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: CreativityNeuro 是一种无需数据的对比权重引导方法，通过在权重空间进行操控来增强大语言模型的发散思维能力，在多项创造力测试中显著提升原创性、惊喜度和创造力，同时有效减少模式坍塌，且无需重新训练或微调。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大语言模型在开放性问题中倾向于生成相似回答，存在"人工蜂巢思维效应"（模式坍塌），严重制约了其在创造性任务中的发散思维能力。现有方法多依赖行为数据或梯度微调，亟需一种无需数据、即插即用的通用解决方案。

Method: 提出 CreativityNeuro，一种无数据的对比权重引导方法。核心思想是在权重空间（而非激活空间）对模型参数施加对比引导，通过操控模型权重来增强发散思维。该方法无需行为数据、无需重新训练，也无需基于梯度的微调。

Result: 在三个任务上验证：(1) DAT词汇空间创造力测试中，性能提升高达14个人类百分位点；(2) 在720人规模的人类评估中，AUT和Task Task任务上的原创性、惊喜度和创造力均显著提升；(3) 三个任务上均显著减少模式坍塌指标。此外，激活引导方法仅在DAT上达到可比性能，但无法迁移至AUT和Task Task，凸显了权重空间引导在任务泛化上的优势。

Conclusion: CreativityNeuro 在无需行为数据、重训练或梯度微调的前提下，有效增强了LLM的发散思维能力并减少了模式坍塌，为提升模型在创造性领域的表现提供了一种简洁高效的方案。

Abstract: Divergent thinking is a crucial aspect of creativity, yet large language models (LLMs) tend to consistently generate similar responses to open-ended questions, in what has been termed the artificial hivemind effect. Here, we introduce CreativityNeuro, a data-free method for enhancing divergent thinking in LLMs via contrastive weight steering. We evaluate our method across multiple creativity assessments and report several main findings. On the Divergent Association Task (DAT), a vocabulary-space creativity test, CreativityNeuro improves performance by up to 14 human percentile points. Next, in a large-scale human evaluation (N=720) on the Alternative Uses Test (AUT) and the Task Task, CreativityNeuro achieves significant improvements in originality, surprise, and creativity, transferring to longer-form and more open-ended tasks. Importantly, we find that across all three tasks, CreativityNeuro demonstrably reduces measures of mode collapse. Moreover, activation steering achieves comparable performance to CreativityNeuro on the DAT, but it does not transfer to the AUT and Task Task, demonstrating the effectiveness of weight-space steering in generalizing to unseen tasks. In conclusion, CreativityNeuro improves divergent thinking and reduces mode collapse without requiring behavioral data, re-training, or gradient-based fine-tuning, providing a straightforward way to enhance LLM performance in creative domains.

</details>


### [45] [Discrete Diffusion Language Models for Interactive Radiology Report Drafting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01436)
*Max Van Puyvelde,Halil Ibrahim Gulluk,Wim Van Criekinge,Olivier Gevaert*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文首次将扩散语言模型（DiffusionGemma-26B）应用于医学视觉问答，与同规模自回归模型在相同LoRA微调设置下对比，扩散模型在各项指标上达到或超越自回归模型，且解码速度提升3.5-4.4倍，同时具备自回归模型所缺乏的任意顺序文本填充（any-order infill）能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前医学基础模型几乎全部采用自回归（AR）生成方式，而扩散语言模型已在通用文本生成领域表现出竞争力。作者希望探索扩散语言模型在医学领域的潜力，验证其是否能替代自回归范式，并展现扩散模型独有的双向去噪特性在医学报告编写中的实际优势。

Method: 采用混合专家（MoE）架构的扩散语言模型 DiffusionGemma-26B，与同规模自回归模型 Gemma-4-26B 在相同 LoRA 微调设置下进行对比实验。在多个医学视觉问答数据集上评估，使用对冗余表达具有鲁棒性的 LLM 作为评判器进行打分。微调后模型活跃参数仅3.8B。同时展示了扩散模型的任意顺序填充（any-order infill）能力：放射科医生可固定报告片段，让模型填充中间文本。

Result: 扩散模型在所有数据集上匹配或超过自回归模型性能；微调后的模型（3.8B活跃参数）与前沿视觉-语言模型具有竞争力；解码速度比自回归模型快3.5-4.4倍；成功展示了任意顺序填充能力，适合处理不同临床医生和机构间报告风格不一致的现实场景。

Conclusion: 扩散语言模型在医学领域不仅性能可与自回归模型媲美甚至更优，还带来了速度优势和独特的双向填充能力，为医学报告生成和编辑提供了更灵活高效的方案，有望推动医学基础模型从单一自回归范式向扩散范式拓展。

Abstract: Diffusion language models, which generate text by denoising a token canvas bidirectionally instead of emitting tokens left to right, have become competitive with autoregressive (AR) generation. Medical foundation models, however, remain almost entirely autoregressive. We adapt a mixture-of-experts diffusion language model, DiffusionGemma-26B, and benchmark it against its same-size AR sibling Gemma-4-26B under an identical LoRA recipe on medical visual question answering datasets, scored by a verbosity-robust LLM judge. Diffusion matches or exceeds AR on all of them, and the finetuned model (3.8B active) is competitive with frontier vision-language models; its decoding is also 3.5-4.4x faster. Beyond this parity, the diffusion model offers a drafting capability AR lacks: any-order infill. Because the canvas is denoised bidirectionally, a radiologist can fix report fragments and have the model fill the text between them, an operation inherent to diffusion but not to autoregression, which is subpar at it. This suits real reports, which are often terse or inconsistent across clinicians and institutions.

</details>


### [46] [Beyond Next-Token Prediction: An RLVR Proof of Concept for Tool-Use Agents on Atlassian Workflows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01465)
*Karthikeya Aditya Vissa,Sankalp Mane,Ananya Mantravadi,Harshit Rajgarhia,Abhishek Mukherji*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 针对企业SaaS工作流中LLM因训练目标（下一token预测）与实际API调用需求不匹配导致的静默失败问题，论文探索使用可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）直接在目标环境中训练，在模拟Jira和Confluence API的五个合成环境上实验，证明RL训练策略平均奖励从0.35–0.92提升至0.95–1.00，定位为面向小众企业API的结果优化小模型的初步步骤。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型训练目标是预测下一个token，而非在特定API内部正确执行操作。在企业SaaS工作流中，成功意味着按正确顺序、携带正确嵌套参数命中正确端点。这种目标错位导致静默失败：必填字段缺失、工具幻觉、单次读取后过早停止。现有方法缺乏直接在目标环境中以可验证方式进行优化的方案。

Method: 构建五个合成环境，以模式级（schema-level）保真度模拟Jira REST v3和Confluence v2 API。奖励完全由工具调用轨迹（tool-call trace）计算得出，无需在线API、无需学习型评判模型、无需人工标注。在相同检验器上对prompted基线模型（Qwen3-1.7B和Qwen3.5-4B）进行评分，并采用GRPO（Group Relative Policy Optimization）进行强化学习训练，使用可验证奖励（RLVR）。

Result: 在四个奖励非退化（non-degenerate）的场景中，RL训练策略将平均奖励从4B基线的0.35–0.92范围提升至0.95–1.00。其中最大单次提升出现在Confluence页面创建任务（0.35→1.00）。五个场景中有一个（工单状态转换）奖励已饱和，prompted 4B模型已达上限。

Conclusion: RLVR能有效弥合LLM的token预测目标与企业API精确调用需求之间的差距，在合成环境中几乎消除静默失败。但存在两个关键局限：手工构建可验证奖励无法规模化扩展至更多端点；部分场景基线模型已饱和。该工作定位为面向小众企业API的结果优化小模型的初步探索。

Abstract: Large language models are trained to predict the next token, not to act inside a specific API. In niche enterprise SaaS workflows -- where success means hitting the right endpoint with the right nested arguments in the right order -- this objective mismatch shows up as silent failures: dropped required fields, hallucinated tools, or early stops after a single read. We ask whether Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR), applied directly in the target environment, closes the gap. As a proof of concept we build a suite of five synthetic environments emulating the Jira REST v3 and Confluence v2 APIs at schema fidelity; rewards are computed entirely from the tool-call trace, with no live API, no learned judge, and no human label in the loop. Scoring prompted Qwen3-1.7B and Qwen3.5-4B on the same checkers that drive GRPO training, we find that on the four scenarios whose rewards are non-degenerate the RL-trained policy lifts average reward from a 4B-baseline range of 0.35--0.92 to 0.95--1.00, with the largest single gain on Confluence page creation ($0.35 \rightarrow 1.00$). We position this as a preliminary step toward outcome-optimised small models for niche enterprise APIs, and foreground two limitations a workshop reader should weigh: hand-crafting verifiable rewards does not scale beyond the handful of endpoints reported here, and one of our five scenarios (ticket-transition) has a saturating reward shape that the prompted 4B already maxes out.

### [47] [World Feedback for Clinical Agents: Diagnosing RL in FHIR Environments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01470)
*Ananya Mantravadi,Harshit Rajgarhia,Prasanna Desikan,Abhishek Mukherji*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该论文针对临床协议执行任务中的强化学习（RL）训练进行了系统性审计。作者发现现有基准MedAgentBench v1/v2存在41.7%的"静默终止"天花板，导致"不行动"成为RL最优策略。为此，他们构建了MedAgentBench-v3（508个任务，天花板降至8.9%），并通过训练Qwen3-8B揭示了两个结构性障碍：能力天花板（10/20任务类型零基础性能）和格式知识障碍（3/20任务类型需精确临床编码，无法通过探索发现）。纯RL仅达18.2% pass@1，而基于规则的SFT达34.1%，15.9个百分点的差距完全归因于上述障碍。论文提出决策/格式知识/查找的三分类法来预测RL可学习性，并给出处方：用SFT注入编码，用RL学习条件判断。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 临床协议执行任务（如检查化验值、应用阈值、生成FHIR订单）天然适合从世界反馈中进行RL训练，因为临床专家可将决策逻辑编码为验证器，无需逐情节标注即可对无限次rollout打分。然而，实际应用RL需要可靠的反馈通道和足够的基础能力。现有基准存在的"静默终止"问题使得RL训练失效（智能体学会什么都不做即可获得奖励），因此需要审计现有基准并识别阻碍RL成功应用的结构性障碍。

Method: 1）审计MedAgentBench v1/v2，量化"静默终止天花板"问题；2）构建MedAgentBench-v3（508个任务），通过收紧奖励设计和验证逻辑将天花板从41.7%降至8.9%；3）在Qwen3-8B上开展RL训练实验，系统分析20种任务类型的表现；4）识别两类结构性障碍（能力天花板和格式知识障碍），并据此提出决策/格式知识/查找三分类法来预测RL可学习性；5）对比纯RL与基于规则的SFT方法，验证分类法的解释力。

Result: 1）MedAgentBench v1/v2存在41.7%的静默终止天花板，使"不行动"成为RL优势策略；2）MAB-v3将天花板降至8.9%；3）Qwen3-8B在20种任务类型中，10种基础性能为0%（零梯度），3种需要精确临床编码且无法通过探索发现；4）纯RL达到18.2% pass@1，基于规则的SFT达34.1%，差距15.9个百分点；5）该差距完全由上述两种结构性障碍解释；6）三分类法有效预测了各任务类型的RL可学习性。

Conclusion: RL在临床协议执行任务中的成功应用受到两类结构性障碍的制约：能力天花板（基础模型在某些任务类型上完全无法起步）和格式知识障碍（精确临床编码无法通过探索发现）。论文提出的决策/格式知识/查找三分类法为这些障碍提供了统一的解释框架，并指明了解决方案：使用SFT注入编码知识（解决格式知识障碍），使用RL学习条件判断逻辑（发挥RL优势）。这种混合策略有望在实际临床智能体训练中发挥关键作用。

Abstract: Clinical protocol-execution tasks -- checking a lab value, applying a threshold, placing a correctly structured FHIR order -- are natural candidates for RL from world feedback: once clinical SMEs encode decision logic into a verifier, that verifier grades unlimited rollouts without per-episode annotation. But applying RL requires a sound feedback channel and sufficient base capability. We audit MedAgentBench v1/v2, find a 41.7\% silent-finish ceiling that makes inaction the RL dominant strategy, and construct \textbf{MedAgentBench-v3 (MAB-v3)} (508 tasks, 8.9\% ceiling). Training Qwen3-8B exposes two structural barriers: a \emph{capability ceiling} (10/20 task types have 0\% base performance, zero gradient) and a \emph{format-knowledge barrier} (3/20 types require exact clinical codes undiscoverable by exploration). Pure RL reaches 18.2\% pass@1 vs.\ 34.1\% for rule-based SFT; the 15.9~pp gap is attributable entirely to these barriers. A decision/format-knowledge/lookup taxonomy predicts RL learnability and prescribes the fix: SFT to inject codes, RL to learn conditionals.

### [48] [Procedural Memory Distillation: Online Reflection for Self-Improving Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01480)
*Ye Liu,Srijan Bansal,Bo Pang,Yang Li,Zeyu Leo Liu,Yifei Ming,Zixuan Ke,Shafiq Joty,Semih Yavuz*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种过程性记忆蒸馏方法（PMD），通过提取和蒸馏跨回合的过程性信号，将策略生成的经验转化为可复用的记忆，并以协同进化框架将其内化到策略参数中，在科学知识和代码生成基准上显著优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有强化学习与可验证奖励方法（如RLVR、SDPO）仅利用回合级别的验证信号，丢弃了rollout中丰富的过程性信息。模型反复遇到相关问题，产生了跨回合信号（哪些策略持续通过验证、哪些失败模式持续存在、哪些模式反复出现），但这些信号无法被回合局部更新所捕获。

Method: PMD在三个抽象层级组织记忆：原始轨迹、自我反思的策略与教训、以及跨问题反复出现的高层行为模式，均为在线从模型自身轨迹中提取。设计了一个记忆条件化的自我教师，利用积累的经验对学生模型的rollout进行监督，使学生逐步将过程性知识内化到参数中。核心设计原则是协同进化：策略生成rollout更新记忆，记忆塑造监督来更新策略。

Result: 在Qwen3-8B和OLMo3-Instruct-7B上，PMD相比SDPO在SCIKNOWEVAL上提升3.8-5.5%，在LIVECODEBENCH上提升7.9-13.6%。消融实验表明，冻结记忆或策略均会导致SCIKNOWEVAL各领域性能下降超过10%，验证了协同进化的关键作用。

Conclusion: PMD通过保留和蒸馏跨回合过程性信号，有效弥补了回合级更新的不足。协同进化设计使记忆作为训练脚手架被策略吸收，推理时无需额外记忆模块，实现了高效且可扩展的过程性知识内化。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR), along with recent selfdistillation variants such as SDPO, evaluates each rollout against a verifier and updates the policy from that episode-level signal. However, the richer procedural information in the rollout is rarely retained or reused. Across episodes and epochs, the model repeatedly encounters related problems under a changing policy, producing cross-episode signals that episode-local updates cannot capture: which strategies consistently pass verification, which failure modes persist, which patterns recur. We propose Procedural Memory Distillation (PMD), which converts these crossepisode signals into reusable procedural memory and distills it into the policy's weights during training. This memory functions as a training scaffold, absorbed into the policy itself, yielding a memory-free model at inference. PMD organizes the memory at three levels of abstraction: raw trajectories, self-reflected strategies and lessons, and higher-level behavioral patterns that recur across problems, all extracted online from the model's own trajectories. A memory-conditioned self-teacher draws on the accumulated experience to supervise the student on its own rollouts, enabling student to progressively internalize procedural knowledge within its parameters. The central design principle is co-evolution: the policy generates rollouts that update the memory, and memory shapes the supervision that updates the policy. Empirically, across Qwen3-8B and OLMo3-Instruct-7B, PMD improves over SDPO by 3.8-5.5% on SCIKNOWEVAL and 7.9-13.6% on LIVECODEBENCH. Co-evolution powers these gains: freezing either the memory or the policy trails PMD by more than 10% across SCIKNOWEVAL domains.

</details>


### [49] [The Agentic Garden of Forking Paths](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01507)
*Jiacheng Miao,Jonathan K Pritchard,James Zou*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文揭示了科学研究中“分叉路径”问题——同一数据因不同分析选择可得出截然相反的结论。AI代理能够通过分配不同“人设”复现这种分析变异，并使其显式化。在移民数据研究中，AI代理复现了72%的人类意识形态差异，且86%的AI报告通过AI评审、78%通过人类专家评审，说明问题不在分析缺陷，而在选择性探索与报告。为此，作者提出m值（多元宇宙值）和Agentic Bootstrap方法，用于评估单一报告分析在整个合理分析分布中的位置，将这一分布转化为科学可信度的评判标准。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实证研究中，同一数据可因不同分析路径得出不同甚至相反的结论，但这些“分叉路径”通常是隐蔽的。作者旨在揭示这一问题的系统性，并利用AI代理使分析路径显式化，进而提出量化评估科学证据可信度的新方法。

Method: 1. 在四个高风险领域，为AI代理分配不同“人设”（personas），使其对同一数据和问题生成分析路径并输出结论；2. 在42个人类研究团队分析过的移民数据集上，用AI代理复现分析，比较AI与人类在意识形态维度上的效应估计差异；3. 对AI生成的报告进行AI评审和人类专家评审；4. 提出m值（multiverse value）——某分析路径产生至少同等极端结论的概率；5. 提出Agentic Bootstrap方法，利用AI代理采样合理的分析路径空间以估计m值。

Result: 1. AI代理通过人设分配即可对同一数据得出系统性分歧的结论，且结论与该人设的信念一致；2. 在移民研究中，AI代理复现了72%的人类意识形态差异；3. 86%的AI报告通过AI评审，78%通过人类多数专家评审，表明单篇报告难以识别明显缺陷；4. 将Agentic Bootstrap应用于人类移民研究，13.5%的人类报告分析落在分析空间最极端的5%范围内（m<0.05）。

Conclusion: 科学证据的核心挑战并非分析本身有缺陷，而是从大量方法学上可辩护的分析中进行选择性探索与报告。AI代理使这种探索廉价且可规模化，可能放大这一长期问题。科学证据的可信度不应仅凭单一报告分析来判断，还应评估其在合理分析分布中的位置。Agentic Bootstrap使这一分布可观测，并将其转化为科学可信度的评判标准。

Abstract: Empirical research rarely admits a unique analysis. Different analytical choices can lead to different conclusions from the same data, yet these hidden forking paths are difficult to observe. We show that AI agents capture much of the analytical variation among human researchers while making these paths explicit. Across four high-stakes domains, assigning different personas is sufficient for AI agents to report divergent, often opposing, conclusions from the same data and question, with findings systematically aligned with those beliefs. In a study in which 42 human research teams analyzed the same immigration dataset, AI agents reproduced 72% of the human ideological gap in reported effect estimates. Despite reaching opposing conclusions, it is difficult to identify clear issues in each analysis based on the final AI reports: 86% passed independent AI review and 78% passed majority human expert review. These findings suggest that the central challenge is often not flawed analyses, but selective exploration and reporting from a large space of methodologically defensible analyses. AI agents may amplify this longstanding problem by making such exploration inexpensive and scalable. To address this, we introduce the m-value (multiverse value), the probability that an analysis path would produce a claim at least as extreme as the reported one. We further introduce Agentic Bootstrap, which estimates the m-value by using AI agents to sample plausible analysis paths. Applied to the human immigration study, 13.5% of reported human analyses fell in the most extreme 5% of the analysis space (m<0.05). Scientific evidence should therefore be evaluated not only by a single reported analysis but also by its position within the distribution of analyses that could reasonably have been reported. Agentic Bootstrap makes this distribution observable and turns it into a criterion for scientific credibility.

</details>


### [50] [Janus: a Playground for User-Involved Agentic Permission Management](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01510)
*Natalie Grace Brigham,Eugene Bagdasarian,Tadayoshi Kohno,Franziska Roesner*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: Janus 是一个用于设计和评估用户参与式智能体权限管理的系统，包含模块化核心框架 Janus-Core 和自动化评估框架 Janus-Harness。通过在六个权限助手上进行多场景实验，研究表明用户输入对隐私安全至关重要，AI 增强决策可降低认知负担，但需考虑权限疲劳等现实行为，且不存在适用于所有场景的最优设计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自主执行工具调用的 AI 智能体引发了权限管理的核心问题：用户应扮演什么角色？尽管已有多种方案被提出，但智能体权限管理中用户的参与角色仍未得到充分探索。

Method: 提出 Janus 系统，包含两部分：(1) Janus-Core：模块化智能体系统，支持多样化权限管理设计；(2) Janus-Harness：自动化评估框架。基于识别用户参与关键设计轴的概念模型，在完整设计空间中实现了六种权限助手，并在三个场景和三个合成响应者上进行评估。

Result: 实验表明：(1) 用户输入至关重要，能显著增强隐私与安全性；(2) AI 对用户决策的增强有助于降低认知负担；(3) 系统设计必须考虑权限疲劳等现实用户行为；(4) 不存在在所有上下文中最优的单一设计。

Conclusion: 在智能体系统中部署权限助手需要采用更具原则性和上下文敏感的方法。Janus 已公开发布，以支持该方向的进一步研究。

Abstract: AI agents that autonomously execute tool calls on a user's behalf raise pressing questions about permission management: what role could users play, and what role should they play? Despite many proposed approaches, the user's role in agentic permission management remains under explored. We introduce Janus, a playground system for implementing and evaluating user-involved agentic permission management designs. Janus consists of two components: Janus-Core, a modular agentic system supporting a diverse spectrum of permission management designs, and Janus-Harness, an automated evaluation framework. Grounded in a conceptual model that identifies key design axes for user involvement, we implement six permission assistants spanning the design space and evaluate them across three scenarios and three synthetic responders. We demonstrate that user input is critical and can significantly strengthen privacy and security, that AI augmentation of user decisions can help reduce cognitive load, and that realistic user behavior including permission fatigue must be accounted for in system design. No single design performs optimally across all contexts, motivating a more principled and context-sensitive approach to deploying permission assistants in agentic systems. Janus is publicly available to support future investigation into this dimension of agentic system design.

### [51] [Revisiting Chain-of-Thought Reasoning under Limited Supervision: Semi-supervised Chain-of-Thought Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01511)
*Hongyang He,Jiuming Liu,Victor Sanchez*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出Semi-CoT框架，利用未标注问题生成伪思维链，通过答案级语义熵筛选低熵推理链作为可靠伪监督信号，将CoT从推理时提示扩展为半监督学习范式。实验显示熵门控可筛选高精度伪CoT（91%-100%），但下游增益有限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有CoT方法仅在推理时使用推理链作为提示，生成的推理轨迹很少被复用为半监督学习信号。作者希望利用大量未标注问题构建伪推理监督，将CoT的自训练视角从推理时优化扩展至半监督伪监督学习。

Method: 提出Semi-CoT框架：(1)对每个未标注问题采样多条伪CoT推理链；(2)计算答案级语义熵以估计推理链的不确定性；(3)通过熵门控选择低熵推理链作为可靠伪CoT示范；(4)将筛选后的伪CoT用于学生模型的半监督训练。

Result: 在AQuA、SVAMP、GSM8K、MultiArith四个数据集上的实验表明：熵门控筛选的伪答案精度在91.36%到100%之间；SVAMP和GSM8K上获得小幅提升，AQuA出现负迁移，MultiArith达到性能上限。

Conclusion: 未标注问题可提供可靠的伪推理信号，但有效利用这些信号仍需更强的示范选择策略或更好的学生训练方法。

Abstract: Chain-of-thought (CoT) reasoning has emerged as an effective approach for activating latent reasoning capabilities in large language models. However, most existing CoT methods use reasoning chains mainly as inference-time prompts, while the generated reasoning traces are rarely reused as semi-supervised learning signals. In this report, we define \textbf{Semi-supervised Chain-of-Thought Learning} and propose \textbf{Semi-CoT}, a simple framework that uses unlabeled questions to construct pseudo reasoning supervision. Semi-CoT samples multiple pseudo-CoTs for each unlabeled question, estimates answer-level semantic entropy, and selects low-entropy reasoning chains as reliable pseudo-CoT demonstrations. This extends the self-training view of CoT from inference-time refinement to semi-supervised pseudo-supervision. Pilot experiments on AQuA, SVAMP, GSM8K, and MultiArith show that the entropy gate selects high-precision pseudo-CoTs, with pseudo-answer precision ranging from $91.36\%$ to $100\%$. Semi-CoT also gives small gains on SVAMP and GSM8K, while AQuA shows negative transfer and MultiArith reaches a ceiling. These results suggest that unlabeled questions can provide reliable pseudo reasoning signals, but their effective use still requires stronger demonstration selection or student training.

### [52] [OPINE-World: Programmatic World Modeling with Ontology-error-Prioritized Interactive Exploration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01531)
*David Courtis,Wenhao Li,Scott Sanner*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: OPINE-World 提出了一种在线学习的对象中心程序化世界模型，通过假设-检验循环中的双智能体协作（环境交互与代码合成），结合本体误差驱动的探索策略，在 ARC-AGI-3 基准上以零游戏专项训练的方式解决了 25 款游戏中的 20 款，动作效率得分达 78.4。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出 OPINE-World 系统，核心机制包括：(1) 双智能体协作架构——一个智能体在环境中执行动作，另一个智能体通过重放验证和基于模型的规划进行代码合成；(2) 假设-检验循环，持续迭代优化程序化世界模型；(3) 本体误差（ontology error），一种贝叶斯度量的对象类型充分性指标，用于引导探索行为；(4) 在线学习范式，无需预定义对象词汇表，从交互中灵活推断对象结构。

Result: 在 ARC-AGI-3 基准（一个隐藏对象词汇、目标和动作语义的技能习得效率测试平台）上，OPINE-World 在 25 款游戏中解决了 20 款，且无需逐游戏训练；动作效率得分达到 78.4，可与人类基线相比拟。

Conclusion: OPINE-World 证明了通过双智能体假设-检验架构与本体误差驱动的探索，程序化世界模型可以成功扩展到像素渲染环境，实现了数据高效、可复用且具备灵活对象结构推断能力的在线世界模型学习。

Abstract: Learning how an environment behaves from interaction is central to building agents that adapt to unfamiliar tasks. World models learned with deep networks are flexible but data-hungry and transfer poorly beyond their training distribution. Program-synthesized world models, written as source code by LLMs and refined through counterexample-guided inductive synthesis (CEGIS), are instead data-efficient and reusable, yet they have been demonstrated mainly on structured-state worlds with a given object vocabulary, and a single program search does not scale to pixel-rendered environments whose object structure must be hypothesized flexibly. We introduce OPINE-World, an LLM agent that learns an object-centric programmatic world model online from interaction. OPINE-World couples two cooperating agents in a loop of hypothesis and test, one acting in the environment and one synthesizing the model in code with replay verification and model-based planning, and it steers exploration with a Bayesian measure of object-type adequacy we call ontology error. We evaluate OPINE-World on ARC-AGI-3, a benchmark for skill-acquisition efficiency in which the object vocabulary, the goal, and the action semantics are withheld. OPINE-World solves 20 of 25 games without per-game training and reaches an action-efficiency score of 78.4 against the human baseline.

### [53] [Scaling Trends for Lie Detector Oversight in Preference Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01567)
*Oskar J. Hollinsworth,Ann-Kathrin Dombrowski,Sam Adam-Day,Adam Gleave,Chris Cundy*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文扩展了SOLiD（通过测谎器实现可扩展监督）方法，将其应用于更大规模模型和更真实的偏好学习场景。研究发现，随着模型规模扩大，未被检测到的欺骗行为显著下降，且可以在微调阶段完全移除昂贵的人工标注者而不显著增加欺骗。但该方法对分布偏移敏感，可能导致测谎器误报率升高到不可接受的水平。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM中的欺骗行为监控和预防成本高昂，SOLiD方法虽然利用测谎器来筛选需要人工审查的响应，但其在大规模模型和多样化现实场景中的有效性尚未得到充分验证。

Method: 将SOLiD方法扩展到更大参数规模的模型（1B到405B），并在更多样化、更现实的偏好学习设置中进行评估，测试在不同检测器真正率下的未检测欺骗率，以及完全移除微调阶段人工标注者的影响。

Result: 在检测器真正率为99%时，未检测到的欺骗从1B模型的34%降至405B模型的14%，呈现良好的规模扩展特性；完全移除微调阶段的人工标注者后，欺骗率未出现统计显著增加。但检测器训练数据与偏好训练数据之间的分布偏移会导致误报率达到不可接受的水平。

Conclusion: SOLiD在大规模模型上展现出有利的扩展性，人工标注者可被进一步替代，但分布偏移带来的误报率问题是该方法实际部署的关键瓶颈，需在未来工作中解决。

Abstract: Deceptive behavior in LLMs is costly to monitor and prevent, motivating approaches such as Scalable Oversight via Lie Detectors (SOLiD) (Cundy & Gleave, 2025), which uses lie detectors to identify responses for review by high-cost labelers. In this paper, we scale SOLiD to larger models and evaluate it in more diverse and realistic preference-learning settings. We find favorable scaling: undetected deception drops from 34% for 1B-parameter models to 14% for 405B-parameter models at a detector true positive rate of 99%, and expensive human labelers can be removed entirely from the fine-tuning phase without a statistically significant increase in deception. However, SOLiD is sensitive to distribution shift between detector training and preference-training data, which can drive detector false positive rates to impractical levels.

Abstract: Large language models have recently been explored for scientific hypothesis generation, but most prior work relies on unstructured literature and free-form textual claims. We present a pipeline for Earth observation that grounds hypothesis generation directly in the NASA Earth Observation Knowledge Graph. A heterogeneous graph neural network trained on historical co-usage relations ranks candidate dataset pairings, and a three-agent LLM pipeline filters, generates, and evaluates structured research hypotheses. ### [55] [Hawk: Harnessing Hardware-Aware Knowledge for High-Performance NPU Kernel Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01590)
*Junyi Wen,Ruiyan Zhuang,Yongjia Xu,Pengtu Li,Rui Zou,Hongyi Chen,Chingman Wan,Puxu Yang,Wuhui Chen,Yanlin Wang*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前 LLM 在 NPU 内核开发中因缺乏硬件特定先验知识而频繁失败——简单移植代码虽能通过编译，却会因隐式违反硬件约束而导致运行时崩溃和性能退化，亟需一种能注入硬件感知知识的自动化方案。

Method: 提出 Hawk 框架，包含三大核心模块：(1) 运行时知识合成模块，采用三元组可执行知识表示，将错误上下文与可执行语义内在耦合；(2) 瓶颈感知知识检索模块，实现二维检索范式，将查询投影到正交的语法空间与硬件对齐的语义空间；(3) 效果驱动知识蒸馏模块，基于实证执行反馈，利用 LLM 语义仲裁持续剪除错误、合并冗余来蒸馏知识。

Result: 在真实 NPU 工作负载上的广泛评估表明，Hawk 将生成准确率从 49.4% 提升至 80.0%，执行速度相较 SOTA 基线最高达 2.2 倍加速。

Conclusion: Hawk 通过训练无关的硬件感知知识管理机制，有效解决了 LLM 在 NPU 内核生成中的灾难性失败问题，显著提升了生成质量与运行效率。

Abstract: Developing high-performance kernels for Neural Processing Units (NPUs) is a critical industry bottleneck, requiring developers to manually navigate implicit hardware constraints and strict memory hierarchies. While large language models offer immense automation potential, they fail catastrophically on NPUs due to a fundamental lack of hardware-specific priors. Naively transplanting code snippets from similar NPU kernels may pass the compiler, but it consistently triggers runtime crashes and performance degradation by blindly violating underlying hardware constraints. To overcome this, we introduce Hawk, a training-free framework that harnesses hardware-aware knowledge through three core modules: (1) Run-Time Knowledge Synthesis Module, which employs a Triple-Part Executable Knowledge Representation to inherently couple the error context with executable semantics; (2) Bottleneck-Aware Knowledge Retrieval Module, which implements a 2D-Retrieval paradigm to project queries into orthogonal syntactic and hardware-aligned semantic spaces; and (3) Effect-Driven Knowledge Distillation Module, which leverages LLM-driven semantic arbitration to continuously distill the knowledge by pruning errors and consolidating redundancies based on the empirical execution feedback. Extensive evaluations on real-world NPU workloads demonstrate that Hawk elevates generation accuracy from 49.4% to 80.0%, while achieving up to a 2.2x execution speedup over state-of-the-art baselines.

While existing approaches integrate Large Language Models (LLMs) for semantic understanding and Deep Reinforcement Learning (DRL) for policy optimization, they often rely on sequential, loosely coupled architectures that underutilize the generative and reasoning capabilities of LLMs. In this paper, we propose a paradigm shift with PASE, a Planning-Aware Semantic self-healing engine, a novel fault self-healing framework that reconceptualizes recovery as a neuro-symbolic program synthesis task. PASE employs an LLM as a core Plan Synthesis Engine to generate structured recovery plans from a library of semantic primitives. A Neural-Symbolic World Model verifies plan feasibility through simulation, while a Meta-Prompt Optimizer, trained via DRL, learns to generate optimal prompts that guide the LLM's planning process. This tight reason-plan-verify-adapt loop enables dynamic, context-aware recovery strategy generation beyond predefined action spaces. Experiments on a real-world cloud fault injection dataset demonstrate that PASE significantly outperforms state-of-the-art methods, reducing average system recovery time by over 40% and improving fault detection accuracy in unknown fault scenarios. Our framework advances autonomous system management by unifying LLM-based reasoning with model-assisted verification and meta-learned guidance.

### [58] [Profit-Based Counterfactual Explanations for Product Improvement: A Case Study of Manga Sales in Japan](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01610)
*Keita Kinjo,Takeshi Ebina*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于利润最大化的反事实解释框架（PBCE），将反事实解释重新定义为管理/营销场景下的利润优化问题，从而消除了对预设目标值和距离函数的外生依赖，赋予距离项以属性修改成本的经济学含义。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有反事实解释方法存在两个核心缺陷：（1）在回归场景中需要外生指定目标输出值，但目标值的有效性缺乏保障；（2）距离函数的实际解释意义不足。此外，大多数方法聚焦于改变预测结果，而非直接优化决策目标，这与实际决策中需要显式最大化目标函数的诉求脱节。

Method: 将反事实解释建模为利润最大化问题，提出PBCE框架。该框架以利润最大化作为直接优化目标，消除了外生目标设定的需要；同时将距离项重新解释为修改产品属性所付出的成本，为距离度量赋予明确的经济学基础。

Result: PBCE框架无需外生指定目标值即可生成反事实解释，且距离项具备清晰的经济学解释——产品属性修改成本，使反事实解释更贴合实际管理决策场景。

Conclusion: PBCE通过将反事实解释与利润最大化统一建模，弥补了现有方法在目标规范性和距离解释性方面的不足，为管理决策场景下的可解释性应用提供了更具实践价值的框架。

Abstract: Counterfactual explanation (CE) is widely used to enhance the interpretability of machine learning models and support data-driven decision-making based on model predictions. However, existing CE methods typically require two exogenously specified inputs: a desired output value (target) and a distance function that quantifies changes in explanatory variables. In regression settings, neither the validity of target specification nor the practical interpretation of the distance metric has been sufficiently addressed. Furthermore, most existing CE methods focus on altering predictions rather than optimizing a decision objective, even though real-world decision-making often requires explicit objective maximization. To address these limitations, we formulate CE as a profit maximization problem in management and marketing contexts and propose a framework termed profit-based counterfactual explanation (PBCE). PBCE eliminates the need for exogenous target specification by directly maximizing profit as the primary optimization objective. Concurrently, the distance term is reinterpreted as the cost of modifying product attributes, providing a clear and economically grounded interpretation.

*Xuqing Yang,Yi Yuan,Shanzhe Lei,Xuhong Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: C3RL是一种新颖的强化学习算法，通过同时优化回答正确性、置信度校准和数据集参考准确率三个奖励信号，解决LLM在RL训练后校准能力退化的问题。在此基础上，CAS策略利用校准后的置信度自适应分配推理资源，在保持性能的同时最多减少12.33倍推理预算。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有RL奖励设计仅关注回答正确性，忽视了模型对自身预测置信度的准确表达能力，导致模型在不确定时产生过度自信的幻觉。这种"性能提升但校准恶化"的矛盾迫切需要解决，以实现更可信赖的LLM部署。

Method: 提出C3RL算法，在RL训练中融合三类奖励信号：(1) 正确性奖励（Correctness Reward），确保回答准确性；(2) 校准奖励（Calibration Reward），引导模型输出与真实准确率一致的置信度；(3) 数据集参考准确率奖励（Dataset-informed Reference Accuracy Reward），提供先验校准目标。进一步提出CAS策略，在推理阶段根据模型输出的置信度动态分配计算资源（如采样数量），实现自适应测试时扩展。

Result: 在8个文本和多模态数据集上的评估表明，C3RL在提升校准能力的同时不牺牲准确率，超越当前SOTA方法。CAS策略在域内和域外数据集上均优于多数投票，且推理预算最多降低12.33倍。

Conclusion: C3RL与CAS的协同为部署更可靠、资源高效的LLM提供了有效路径。通过置信度校准与自适应推理的结合，有望推动LLM在实际应用中更加可信和高效。

Abstract: Training large language models (LLMs) with reinforcement learning (RL) has significantly advanced their performance on reasoning and question-answering tasks. However, prevailing RL reward designs typically prioritize response correctness, neglecting to incentivize models to express their confidence accurately. This leads to a critical problem: performance gains are often accompanied by poor calibration between confidence and accuracy, misleading models to overconfidently hallucinate when uncertain. To address this limitation, we propose $\textbf{C}$orrectness and $\textbf{C}$onfidence $\textbf{C}$alibration $\textbf{R}$einforcement $\textbf{L}$earning ($\textbf{C3RL}$), a novel RL algorithm integrating correctness, calibration and dataset-informed reference accuracy rewards together. Comprehensive evaluation across 8 text and multimodal datasets demonstrates that C3RL enhances calibration without sacrificing accuracy, outperforming the current state-of-the-art method in both performance and calibration metrics. Utilizing the well-calibrated verbalized confidence from C3RL, we further introduce $\textbf{C}$onfidence-based $\textbf{A}$daptive Test Time $\textbf{S}$caling ($\textbf{CAS}$), an adjustable inference-time strategy that allocates computational resources based on response confidence. Experiments show that CAS surpasses majority voting on both in-domain and out-of-domain datasets while reducing the inference budget by up to 12.33 times. We believe the synergy of C3RL and CAS paves the way for deploying more reliable and resource-efficient LLMs. The code, data and models will be released.

</details>


### [60] [Spatial Support Matters: Geometry-Aware Graph Fusion for Rainfall Field Reconstruction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01621)
*Low Jun Yu,Niramay Kachhadiya,Herath Mudiyanselage Viraj Vidura Herath,Sanka Rasnayaka,Lucy Amanda Marshall*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出一种几何感知的多支持异构GNN，将0D点、1D线、2D网格观测作为不同节点层，通过跨支持消息传递融合多源降雨数据，实现任意目标位置的高分辨率降雨场重建。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有降雨感知系统（雨量计、微波链路、雷达/卫星）具有不兼容的空间支持（点、线、网格），现有异构方法仅在特征空间融合而丢弃了几何结构信息，未能充分利用各观测的空间支撑特性。

Method: 提出几何感知多支持异构图神经网络：按支持类型（0D/1D/2D）将观测建模为不同节点层，通过跨支持消息传递融合信息，并采用归纳式掩码节点公式将预测分辨率与感知分辨率解耦，支持在用户自定义位置重建降雨场。

Result: 在新加坡数据上，RMSE比反距离加权插值基线降低23.2%，持续优于卷积融合和支持无关异构GNN基线。悉尼数据泛化研究表明，融合增益取决于雨量计间距与降雨场空间相关长度的关系：当场欠采样时增益最大，已充分解析时增益甚微。

Conclusion: 几何感知的多支持异构GNN能有效融合不同空间支撑的降雨观测，在欠采样场景下优势显著，为城市洪水建模提供高分辨率降雨场重建方案。

Abstract: Fine-scale rainfall reconstruction is critical for urban flood modeling, but real rainfall sensing systems observe the field through incompatible spatial supports: gauges measure points, microwave links measure paths, and radar/satellite products measure gridded areas. These differences in measurement support impose geometrically distinct constraints on the rainfall field, yet existing heterogeneous graph approaches reconcile such sources in feature space, giving each its own embedding while discarding the geometry of its support. We propose a geometry-aware multi-support heterogeneous graph neural network that represents each observation according to its support type (0D point, 1D line, or 2D grid) as a distinct node layer, and fuses them through cross-support message passing into a point-support prediction layer from which the field is reconstructed. An inductive masked-node formulation decouples prediction resolution from sensing resolution, allowing the same trained model to reconstruct the field at user-defined target locations or display grids. On Singapore data, the proposed method reduces RMSE by 23.2\% over the classical interpolation baseline, inverse-distance weighting, and consistently outperforms other neural architectures such as convolutional fusion and support-agnostic heterogeneous graph baselines. A generalization study using data from Sydney, Australia lets us characterize when multi-support fusion helps: the available skill appears to depend on gauge spacing relative to the spatial correlation length of the field, so fusion delivers the largest gains where the field is under-sampled relative to its correlation length and little when it is already resolved. Code and models will be open-sourced upon paper acceptance.

</details>


### [61] [Autonomous discovery of traffic laws with AI traffic scientists](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01639)
*Xingyuan Dai,Yue Liu,Xiaoyan Gong,Qinghai Miao,Junyou Shang,Yutong Wang,Chao Guo,Yonglin Tian,Yizhang Chai,Chao Xiang,Yisheng Lv,Fei-Yue Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: TrafficSci是一个智能体AI系统，将交通定律发现形式化为迭代、可审计的工作流，整合证据范围界定、批判-评判假设归纳及观测-干预验证，在四个尺度上重新发现三条已知定律，并识别出城市驾驶行为中未被报道的内在时间记忆尺度。

Method: TrafficSci采用智能体AI架构，将交通定律发现构建为迭代可审计的工作流，包含三个核心阶段：(1)证据范围界定——自动收集和筛选多源异构交通数据；(2)批判-评判假设归纳——通过批判生成与评判机制迭代提出候选定律；(3)观测-干预验证——结合观测数据验证与干预实验确认定律的因果性与普适性。

Result: 在覆盖人口、网络、控制与轨迹四个尺度的案例研究中，TrafficSci自主重新发现了三条已确立的交通定律，并识别出一条此前未被报道的规律——城市驾驶行为中存在内在时间记忆尺度，该规律在八个城市和两个轨迹数据集上具有统计一致性。

Conclusion: TrafficSci为将AI驱动的科学发现从受控领域扩展至复杂城市系统提供了一条可行路径，展示了智能体AI在交通科学自动化发现中的潜力。

Abstract: Universal traffic laws describe recurrent patterns in congestion, mobility and driving behavior across cities, providing a scientific basis for transportation planning, management and control. Their discovery, however, remains expert-driven, requiring candidate regularities to be identified from heterogeneous observational evidence or validated through intervention experiments. Although autonomous artificial intelligence (AI) systems have advanced scientific discovery in controlled laboratory settings, extending them to complex transportation domains remains a challenge. Here we present TrafficSci, an agentic AI system that formulates traffic-law discovery as an iterative, auditable workflow integrating evidence scoping, critic-judge hypothesis induction, and observational-interventional validation. Across four case studies spanning population, network, control and trajectory scales, TrafficSci autonomously rediscovers three established traffic laws and identifies an unreported intrinsic temporal memory scale in urban driving behavior, statistically consistent across eight cities and two trajectory datasets. TrafficSci provides a route for extending AI-driven scientific discovery from controlled domains to complex urban systems.

### [62] [Diverse Evidence, Better Forecasts: Multi-Agent Deliberation Under Information Asymmetry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01661)
*Yuante Li,Yicheng Tao,Kate Zhang,Taozhi Wang,Gefei Gu,Yaxin Zhou*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 多智能体预测系统中，若所有代理接收相同证据，讨论会退化为羊群效应。本文提出通过信息不对称设计——将证据划分为共享公共子集和互斥私密子集——来降低代理间误差相关性，并基于此构建了InfoDelphi框架，在PolyGym基准上显著优于单代理和其他多代理基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有多智能体预测系统忽视了信息分配这一关键设计选择：当所有代理接收相同信息时，多代理间的讨论仅沦为相互模仿的羊群效应，而非真正的信念修正，导致多代理系统相比单代理并无实质优势。作者将此识别为一个根本性缺口，旨在通过引入信息不对称来解决该问题。

Method: 提出InfoDelphi框架，核心理念是"设计的信息不对称"：将证据分解为共享的公共子集和各代理互不相交的私密子集，使每个代理掌握独有的知识，必须通过讨论才能传递给他人。理论上证明了这种分解可降低代理间的误差相关性。框架包含三个关键组件：(1) 相关性感知的证据路由，(2) 基于理由的迭代讨论，(3) 置信度加权的聚合机制。在PolyGym基准（375个来自真实预测市场的二元预测问题）上进行评估。

Result: 在PolyGym基准上，InfoDelphi在Brier分数上超越最强单代理和多代理基线12-18%，准确率提升4-8个百分点。消融实验进一步证实，移除信息不对称会消除大部分讨论收益，验证了输入多样性是多智能体推理有效性的关键推动因素。

Conclusion: 信息输入的多样性——而非简单的多代理讨论本身——才是多智能体推理系统有效的核心机制。设计的非对称信息分配是弥合当前多代理系统与真正有效讨论之间鸿沟的关键。

Abstract: Multi-agent systems are increasingly used for forecasting future events, as deliberation among multiple LLMs is believed to improve reasoning and calibration. Yet existing approaches overlook a critical design choice: what information each agent receives. When all agents are given identical evidence, deliberation collapses into herding rather than genuine belief revision, leaving multi-agent systems little better than a single agent. We identify this as a fundamental gap and propose designed information asymmetry to close it: by partitioning evidence into shared public and disjoint private subsets, each agent holds exclusive knowledge that can only reach others through deliberation. We theoretically show that this decomposition reduces inter-agent error correlation, and instantiate it in InfoDelphi, a framework combining relevance-aware evidence routing, rationale-based iterative deliberation, and confidence-weighted aggregation. On PolyGym, a benchmark of 375 binary forecasting questions derived from real-world prediction markets, InfoDelphi outperforms the strongest single-agent and multi-agent baselines by 12--18% in Brier score and 4--8 percentage points in accuracy. More detailed experiments confirm that removing information asymmetry eliminates most deliberation gains, establishing diversity of input as the key enabler of effective multi-agent reasoning.

</details>


### [63] [Separating Expert Retention from Autonomous Source Inference in Raw-ECG-Replay-Free Continual ECG Deployment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01674)
*Yufan Lu,Xinhui Liu,Chenyang Xu,Yuxi Zhou,Hao Wang,Shenda Hong*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于冻结ECGFounder特征的增量式专家库方法，用于多源ECG部署中的持续学习。每个新数据源添加一个线性专家分类器，并利用保留的训练特征训练轻量级路由器进行源推断；同时采用top-2边际融合策略替代硬路由决策，以缓解源推断错误带来的性能损失。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在多源ECG部署场景中，早期原始ECG数据无法保留或回放，模型需要持续整合新数据源。冻结预训练骨干并为每个源分配独立分类器可避免参数干扰，但在推理时缺乏源元数据的情况下，仍需自动选择正确的专家。现有方法在源推断上存在瓶颈，亟需一种无需重放原始数据即可实现增量部署与自主源选择的方案。

Method: 基于冻结的1024维ECGFounder特征，为每个新到达的数据域添加一个balanced-softmax线性专家分类器；同时，仅利用已保留的训练特征和域标签拟合一个轻量级MLP路由器。推理时，采用验证集校准的边际规则融合top-2最可能的专家输出，而非依赖单一路由决策。该方法不重放原始ECG，但保留冻结特征用于路由器更新。

Result: 在CPSC、PTB-XL、Georgia和Chapman-Shaoxing四个数据集上：源已知的专家选择达到Macro-F1 0.7915±0.0036，与离线独立头参考（0.7885±0.0009）相当；无源ID时，MLP路由器达到0.7756±0.0027，top-2边际融合达到0.7782±0.0022。top-2相比硬路由的增益仅为+0.0026，配对bootstrap的95%置信区间包含零。三种域顺序下，top-2到Oracle的差距保持在0.0111–0.0133，表明自主源推断是主要剩余瓶颈。

Conclusion: 冻结骨干+独立专家+路由器的方法在无需重放原始ECG的条件下实现了较强的源感知专家保留能力。Top-2边际融合对路由错误的缓解效果有限，自主源推断仍是制约性能的主要瓶颈。该方法需保留训练特征用于路由器更新，并非完全记忆无关。

Abstract: In multi-source ECG deployment, models may need to incorporate new data sources when earlier raw ECGs cannot be retained or replayed. Freezing a pretrained backbone and assigning each source an isolated classifier prevents parameter interference, but deployment still requires selecting an expert when source metadata are unavailable. We study this distinction through \ours{}, an incremental expert bank built on frozen 1024-dimensional ECGFounder features. Each arriving domain adds a balanced-softmax linear expert, while a lightweight router is fitted only on retained training features and domain labels from sources observed so far. A validation-calibrated margin rule fuses the two most likely experts instead of committing to a single routed expert.
  On CPSC, PTB-XL, Georgia, and Chapman-Shaoxing, source-aware expert selection reaches $0.7915\pm0.0036$ Macro-F1 and a matched offline independent-head reference reaches $0.7885\pm0.0009$, supporting strong source-aware expert retention. Without source IDs, an MLP router reaches $0.7756\pm0.0027$ and top-2 margin fusion reaches $0.7782\pm0.0022$. The top-2 gain over hard MLP routing is small ($+0.0026$), with a 95\% confidence interval from paired bootstrap that includes zero. Across three domain orders, the top-2-to-oracle gap remains $0.0111$--$0.0133$, identifying autonomous source inference as the main remaining bottleneck. No raw ECGs are replayed, but frozen training features are retained for router updates; the method is therefore not memory-free.

</details>


### [64] [Epistemic Goggles: A Pretrained Module that Induces an Epistemic Frame via Gradient Editing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01690)
*Joshua Penman*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文针对语言模型微调中的"否定忽视"（Negation Neglect）现象，提出了一种名为Goggles的梯度干预模块。该模块在LoRA微调过程中编辑梯度，赋予模型特定的"认知框架"（epistemic frame），使模型即使在不带虚构标注的文档上训练后，仍能正确识别虚构内容（准确率约91%），同时保持通用能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 语言模型在微调时存在"否定忽视"问题：即使文档被明确标注为虚构，模型仍会吸收文档中的核心主张为真实信息（仅约9%的情况下能正确识别虚构）。这表明仅靠数据层面的标注不足以防止模型从已知不可信的数据中学习不良行为，亟需一种超越数据层面干预的新方法。

Method: 提出Goggles——一种可学习的梯度干预模块。在监督微调（SFT）过程中，Goggles模块编辑LLM的LoRA梯度，将选定的"认知框架"（如"这是虚构内容"或"这是AI安全评估的一部分"）注入到模型从文档中学习的内容中。Goggles针对给定的基座模型、认知框架和LoRA配置仅需训练一次，之后可冻结应用于未见过的文档。该框架支持多种认知立场，且注入的框架在后续持续微调中具有持久性。

Result: 1. 基线模型在标注为虚构的文档上微调后，仅约9%的情况下能正确识别虚构主张；2. 通过Goggles训练后，模型在不带虚构标注的同一批文档上，约91%的情况下能正确标记内容为虚构；3. GPQA和TruthfulQA基准测试显示模型通用能力持平或优于基线；4. Goggles注入的认知框架在后续"回推式"持续微调中保持稳定，而此前其他干预方法会失效。

Conclusion: Goggles展示了一条可行的路径：在不吸收数据中不良行为的前提下，用已知存在对齐问题的数据进行语言模型训练。该方法通过梯度层面的认知框架注入，有效克服了数据层面标注的"否定忽视"局限，为安全利用多样化数据训练模型提供了新思路。

Abstract: Finetuning a language model on documents that are explicitly annotated as fictional results in a model that still actually believes the documents' core claims, an effect known as Negation Neglect. In our evaluations, models trained on documents prefixed and suffixed with such annotations correctly identify the relevant claims as fictional only about 9% of the time. To address this, we introduce Goggles, a learned module that intervenes on the finetuning gradient rather than the data. During supervised finetuning, a Goggles module edits the gradients an LLM LoRA receives, imparting a chosen epistemic frame (the stance the model takes toward the nature of what it reads) to whatever the documents teach. A Goggles instance is trained once for a given base model, frame, and LoRA configuration, then applied frozen to documents it was never trained on. Trained through Goggles on those same documents, now carrying no fictional annotation, the model flags the content as fictional roughly 91% of the time, while preserving capability (GPQA and TruthfulQA match or exceed baseline). The same architecture supports other frames: a Goggles instance can be trained to treat documents as "part of an AI safety evaluation by Redwood Research" rather than simply as fiction. The imparted frame persists under continued finetuning that pushes back toward the claim, where prior interventions revert. Goggles suggests a path toward training language models on known-misaligned data without absorbing the behaviors that data demonstrates.

</details>


### [65] [COMFYCLAW: Self-Evolving Skill Harnesses for Image Generation Workflows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01709)
*Zongxia Li,Dawei Liu,Fuxiao Liu,Yuhang Zhou,Xiyang Wu,Jingxi Chen,Jing Xie,Xiaomin Wu,Lichao Sun*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: COMFYCLAW 是一个面向 ComfyUI 工作流的智能体技能演化框架，将工作流构建形式化为类型化图编辑，利用区域级 VLM 验证器将视觉失败转化为可操作的修复建议，并通过渐进式技能库将历史轨迹和反馈蒸馏为可复用技能，在图像生成评估中显著优于无技能演化的基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着智能体工作流变得重复化和领域专用化，智能体的记忆与可复用技能变得至关重要——智能体应当能够从先前运行中回忆工作流模式、执行约束和用户偏好。现有方法缺乏将历史经验系统化沉淀为可复用技能的有效机制，尤其在基于工作流的图像生成场景中，这一不足尤为突出。

Method: COMFYCLAW 包含四个核心设计：1）将 ComfyUI 工作流构建形式化为类型化图编辑（typed graph editing）；2）按构建阶段组织工具并自动回滚无效编辑；3）使用区域级 VLM 验证器对生成图像进行诊断，将视觉缺陷转化为可操作的修复建议；4）构建渐进式披露的技能库，将历史轨迹、执行错误及验证器反馈蒸馏为可复用的 Agent Skills，支持技能演化。

Result: 在四个基准划分、三种智能体模型和两种图像骨干网络上，COMFYCLAW 在所有六种智能体配置中均取得了最佳平均图像生成评估分数，显著优于无技能演化的仅验证器基线。人工标注进一步表明，标注者偏好 COMFYCLAW 甚于无技能演化的变体。

Conclusion: 技能演化是提升智能体在重复性视觉工作流构建中可靠性与性能的有效机制。COMFYCLAW 通过将历史经验系统化为可复用技能，为工作流驱动的图像生成任务提供了一种可扩展的智能体增强方案。

Abstract: Agents are increasingly used to construct workflows and assist humans in completing recurring tasks more efficiently. As these workflows become repeated and domain-specific, agent memory and reusable skills become increasingly important: agents should be able to recall workflow patterns, execution constraints, and user preferences from previous runs. We study this problem in workflow-based image generation and introduce COMFYCLAW, an agentic skill evolution harness for controlling ComfyUI workflows. COMFYCLAW formulates workflow construction as typed graph editing, exposes tools organized by construction stage, automatically reverts invalid edits, and uses a region-level vision-language model (VLM) verifier to translate visual failures into actionable repair suggestions. The framework further evolves a progressively disclosed skill library, where trajectories, execution errors, and verifier feedback from previous runs are distilled into reusable Agent Skills. Across four benchmark splits, three agent models, and two image backbones, COMFYCLAW achieves the best average image-generation evaluation score across all six agent configurations, outperforming a verifier-only baseline without skill evolution. Human annotations further show that annotators prefer COMFYCLAW over variants without skill evolution. Our results suggest that skill evolution is an effective mechanism for improving agent reliability and performance in recurring visual workflow construction.

</details>


### [66] [Generic Expert Coverage for Pruning SparseMixture-of-Experts Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01710)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出Generic TB-Coverage方法：(1) 使用WikiText2和C4两种通用语料分别对每个专家进行效用评估；(2) 分别从每个语料中保留高效用专家（固定预算覆盖规则）；(3) 合并各语料保留的专家集合构建最终剪枝掩码。在Qwen1.5-MoE-A2.7B和DeepSeek-MoE-16B-Base上以25%、50%、75%保留率进行实验验证。

Conclusion: 保留跨语料专家覆盖是一种有效的通用数据先验，可在固定剪枝预算且不使用下游校准数据的条件下实现更优的MoE剪枝效果。

Abstract: Sparsely activated Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) language models contain substantial structured redundancy among routed experts, but pruning them without downstream calibration data remains challenging. Existing expert-pruning methods typically rely on a single aggregated importance score, which can bias the retained set toward experts favored by dominant calibration patterns. We propose \textbf{Generic TB-Coverage}, a coverage-aware expert pruning method that uses only generic text corpora (WikiText2 and C4) for calibration. Instead of collapsing expert utility into one score, our method profiles per-expert utility separately on each corpus and enforces a fixed-budget coverage rule that preserves high-utility experts from each corpus before constructing the final pruning mask. Across Qwen1.5-MoE-A2.7B and DeepSeek-MoE-16B-Base at 25\%, 50\%, and 75\% retention budgets, our method improves average accuracy on six common zero-shot benchmarks over random pruning, REAP, and ExpertSparsity, while also reducing perplexity degradation on WikiText2 and C4. The gains are largest under aggressive pruning (25\% and 50\% retain), suggesting that preserving cross-corpus expert coverage is an effective generic-data prior for MoE pruning. Our improvements hold with fixed pruning budgets and no downstream calibration data.

### [67] [Distributionally Robust Listwise Preference Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01715)
*Xudong Wu,Jian Qian,Pangpang Liu,Vaneet Aggarwal,Jiayu Chen*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种面向排序标签不确定性的鲁棒Plackett-Luce偏好优化方法，通过总变差鲁棒化将内层最大化从$K!$枚举降为$O(K\log K)$，在离线与在线大语言模型对齐中均展现出强鲁棒性和理论保证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有偏好优化主要聚焦成对监督，鲁棒性设计停留在数据集/提示/偏好对层面。然而，实际中基于列表的排序标签常因标注不一致、近似平局、有损反馈或奖励模型噪声而存在模糊性，listwise场景下的排序标签不确定性尚未被有效建模和鲁棒化。

Method: 作者提出基于总变差(total variation)的鲁棒Plackett-Luce目标函数：将观察到的排序标签视为名义排序的污染版本，在候选列表条件分布上构造一个TV不确定集，推导出鲁棒损失的精确分解——名义PL损失加上最坏情形PL修正项。关键发现是最坏情形排序可通过将当前隐式得分按升序排列获得，从而使内层最大化从$K!$降至$O(K\log K)$。离线设定下目标凸，用投影随机次梯度可收敛；在线策略诱导设定下证明弱凸性并获得$\widetilde O(ε^{-2})$的Moreau包络平稳性。

Result: 离线实验中，鲁棒修正项在干净标签下基本保持原有性能，在噪声标签下鲁棒性显著提升。在线对齐实验中，该方法使基于奖励模型排序的候选扩展更可靠，同时在奖励模型指标和外部GPT-4评判指标上均有改善。

Conclusion: 提出的TV鲁棒Plackett-Luce目标为listwise偏好优化提供了首个处理排序标签不确定性的可计算鲁棒框架，兼具理论收敛保证和实证效果，在离线与在线LLM对齐中均有效。

Abstract: Existing robust preference optimization for language-model alignment mainly studies pairwise supervision and places robustness at the dataset, prompt, or preference-pair level. We instead study listwise preference optimization under ranking-label uncertainty: given a prompt and a candidate list, the observed ranking over that list may be ambiguous due to annotator inconsistency, near-ties, lossy rankwise feedback, or reward-model noise. We propose a pointwise total-variation robust Plackett--Luce objective that directly robustifies the ranking label conditional on the candidate list. The robust loss admits an exact decomposition into the nominal PL loss plus a worst-case PL correction, and the worst-case ranking is obtained by sorting current implicit scores in ascending order, reducing the inner maximization from $K!$ enumeration to $O(K\log K)$. This tractable structure yields strong offline and online optimization guarantees. In the offline fixed-list setting, the robust objective is convex and projected stochastic subgradient reaches global $ε$-suboptimality with $O(ε^{-2})$ sample complexity. In the online policy-induced setting, where candidate lists are generated by the current policy, we establish weak convexity and $\widetilde O(ε^{-2})$ Moreau-envelope stationarity. Experiments in offline LLM alignment show that the proposed robust correction largely preserves performance under clean labels and improves robustness under noise. In online alignment, it makes reward-model-ranked candidate expansion more reliable and improves both reward-model and external GPT-4 judge metrics.

</details>


### [68] [DRL-CLBA: A Clean Label Backdoor Attack for Speech Classification via DDPG Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01729)
*Yueming Huang,Wenhan Yao,Fen Xiao,Xiarun Chen,Weiping Wen*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有语音分类后门攻击多依赖 poisoned label attack（投毒标签攻击），易被人工数据审查检测。作者希望设计一种干净标签（clean label）且样本特定（sample-specific）的后门攻击，在保持标签正确的前提下实现隐蔽投毒。

Method: 提出 DRL-CLBA 框架：(1) 利用深度音频隐写术将样本特定触发器嵌入源音频，在模型深层潜在空间中创建特征锚点；(2) 使用深度确定性策略梯度（DDPG）强化学习优化目标样本，使其在潜在空间中向触发器锚点靠拢，实现无标签迁移的干净标签投毒。

Result: 在三个数据集和四种 DNN 架构上实验，DRL-CLBA 取得高攻击成功率，并能有效绕过微调（fine-tuning）、剪枝（pruning）和频谱签名（spectral signature）等主流后门防御。

Conclusion: DRL-CLBA 暴露了语音控制系统在干净标签后门攻击下的严重脆弱性，证明即使不修改标签也能实现高效、隐蔽且抗防御的后门攻击，对语音安全领域具有重要警示意义。

Abstract: Deep learning models for speech classification are vulnerable to backdoor attacks, where malicious triggers cause misclassification at inference time. While sample-specific attacks can bypass many defenses, they often rely on poisoned label attack, making them detectable via manual data defense. In this paper, we propose DRL-CLBA, a novel clean label backdoor attack for speech classification that leverages Deep Deterministic Policy Gradient (DDPG) reinforcement learning. We also utilize deep audio steganography to embed sample-specific triggers into source audio, creating feature-space anchors. The proposed reinforcement learning framework effectively optimizes target samples toward trigger-bearing anchor points in the model's deep latent space, enabling label-migration-free poisoning of target samples. Experimental results across three datasets and four different DNNs demonstrate that DRL-CLBA achieves a high attack success rate, effectively bypassing some backdoor defenses. The attack demonstrates strong resistance against fine-tuning, pruning, and spectral signature defenses, exposing critical vulnerabilities in speech-controlled systems.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出元基准测试框架：(1)将452个公开基准映射到41项O*NET广义工作活动，再聚合为38个BIAN银行业务领域；(2)采用乘法加权方案（区分度×覆盖率×时效性），在滚动模型窗口上计算权重，自动抑制饱和的遗留测试集；(3)将这些权重作为K因子缩放系数，嵌入成对Elo锦标赛，生成跨基准可比的工作活动分数，业务领域分数为子活动Elo的加权平均。

Abstract: Public LLM leaderboards optimise for global average performance and do not capture the specific cognitive demands of financial-services work: a model that leads on MMLU-Pro may underperform on document-grounded compliance reasoning, and a coding leader may handle multi-turn customer interactions poorly. We present a meta-benchmarking framework that organises 452 publicly reported benchmarks into 41 O*NET Generalized Work Activities and aggregates those into 38 BIAN banking business domains spanning sales, operations, risk, and support work. A multiplicative weighting scheme (discrimination x coverage x recency), computed over a rolling model window, rewards benchmarks that still separate the best models, are widely reported, and remain in active use, suppressing saturated legacy tests automatically. These weights scale the K-factor in a pairwise Elo tournament, producing cross-benchmark-comparable work-activity scores without raw score normalisation; business-domain scores are weighted averages of the constituent work-activity Elos. We demonstrate the framework on a point-in-time public snapshot covering 288 models across 25 organisations as of June 2026, and describe the methodology, full taxonomy, design decisions, and limitations with the aim of making the approach reproducible for institutions facing similar selection and governance challenges.

### [71] [Path-level Hindsight Instructions for Semantic Exploration in Vision-Language Navigation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01754)
*Sung June Kim,Sangpil Kim,Honglak Lee*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: Phi-Nav 提出了一种三阶段双重监督的在线策略框架，通过事后推理（hindsight reasoning）来对齐语言指令与智能体的实际探索轨迹，从而弥合在线探索中的语义监督缺口，在有限专家演示数据下实现有竞争力的 VLN 性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在线策略探索对于训练鲁棒的视觉-语言导航（VLN）智能体至关重要，但探索产生的轨迹往往会偏离专家演示，导致视觉流与原始语言指令之间的语义失配，形成语义监督缺口。

Method: Phi-Nav 采用三阶段双重监督循环：(1) 智能体在专家动作反馈引导下进行在线策略探索并采样轨迹；(2) 事后说话者（hindsight speaker）基于收集的视觉观测合成路径级事后指令；(3) 智能体执行第二次模仿学习，将合成的轨迹-指令对作为额外的专家演示进行训练。

Result: 在 R2R-CE 和 RxR-CE 基准上的评估表明，Phi-Nav 仅需当前基线方法所需专家演示的一小部分，即可取得有竞争力的性能。

Conclusion: 语义探索在 VLN 中不可或缺，Phi-Nav 为在有限数据条件下训练具身智能体提供了一种有效的解决方案。

Abstract: On-policy exploration is a crucial component for training robust Vision-Language Navigation agents, as it exposes the policy to a broader state distribution. However, such exploration inevitably leads to trajectories that deviate from expert demonstrations, resulting in a semantic mismatch between the executed visual stream and the original language instruction. In this work, we address this challenge by introducing Phi-Nav, a unified on-policy framework that leverages hindsight reasoning to align instructions with the agent's actual exploratory journey. Specifically, Phi-Nav operates through a three-stage dual-supervision cycle: 1) the agent performs oracle-guided on-policy exploration, sampling a trajectory while learning from expert action feedback, 2) a hindsight speaker synthesizes a path-level hindsight instruction grounded in the collected visual observations, and 3) the agent conducts a second imitation pass, treating the synthesized trajectory-instruction pair as an additional expert demonstration. Through this process, Phi-Nav bridges the critical semantic supervision gap inherent in on-policy methods, transforming semantically unlabeled movement into dense training signals. Evaluations on the R2R-CE and RxR-CE benchmarks show that Phi-Nav yields competitive performance while requiring only a fraction of the expert demonstrations used by current baselines. These results underscore the necessity of semantic exploration in VLN, positioning Phi-Nav as an effective solution for training embodied agents with limited data.

### [72] [Mastermind: Strategy-grounded Learning for Repository-Scale Vulnerability Reproduction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01764)
*Mingzhe Du,Luu Anh Tuan,Tianyi Wu,Renyang Liu,Zhijiang Guo,Dong Huang,See-Kiong Ng*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出 Mastermind，一个双循环框架，将可迁移的策略学习与任务特定经验分离。通过对高层策略而非完整行动轨迹进行 SFT 和基于里程碑的 GRPO 训练，Mastermind 在 CyberGym 仓库级漏洞复现任务上达到 84.5% 的通过率，显著超越现有方法，且同一策略规划器可迁移提升多个不同的执行器。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有 LLM agent 在仓库级漏洞复现任务中的瓶颈并非单步执行能力不足，而是策略选择错误——即选择了错误的高层方法来完成任务。作者认为，策略（strategy）作为学习单元比完整行动轨迹更紧凑可优化、更具体可指导执行、更稳定可跨尝试复用，因此应将策略学习与具体执行分离。

Method: 提出 Mastermind 双循环框架：(1) 策略循环——训练一个可学习的规划器，通过监督微调（SFT）和基于里程碑的群体相对策略优化（Milestone-based GRPO）学习可复用的漏洞复现策略；(2) 经验循环——维护任务局部策略记录，指导后续尝试。规划器独立于执行器训练，策略学习可提升多个冻结执行器的表现而无需修改其行动生成能力。

Result: 在 CyberGym 的 260 个训练任务和 200 个留出评估任务上，以 GPT-5.5 为冻结执行器时，Mastermind 达到 84.5% 的通过率，优于开放手册 PoC 上下文（60.0%）、Best-of-8 采样（63.0%）和迭代改进（77.0%）。同一规划器还将 GPT-5.4 mini 从 45.0% 提升至 60.0%，将 GLM 5.1 从 58.5% 提升至 71.0%。

Conclusion: 学习高层策略是提升仓库级软件工程 agent 的有效且可迁移的机制。将策略与执行分离的架构设计使策略规划器具备跨模型、跨执行器的泛化能力，为构建更强大的 SE agent 提供了新方向。

Abstract: Repository-level vulnerability reproduction is a demanding software engineering (SE) task: an agent must inspect a codebase, infer the input grammar that reaches a vulnerable path, construct a proof-of-conceptv(PoC), and verify that the crash disappears on the patched build. Recent LLM agents can often execute these steps when the approach is correct, yet they still fail by choosing the wrong strategy. This paper argues that strategy, rather than the full action trajectory, is the right learning unit for such SE agents: it is compact enough to optimize, concrete enough to guide execution, and stable enough to store and reuse across attempts. We present Mastermind, a dual-loop framework that separates transferable strategy learning from task-specific experience. A trainable planner learns reusable vulnerability-reproduction strategies through SFT and milestone-based GRPO, while an experience loop maintains task-local strategy records that guide subsequent attempts. The planner is trained independently of the executor, allowing strategy learning to improve multiple frozen executors without modifying their action-generation capability. We evaluate Mastermind on CyberGym using 260 training tasks and 200 held-out evaluation tasks. With GPT-5.5 as the frozen executor, Mastermind achieves an 84.5% pass rate, outperforming open-book PoC context (60.0%), Best-of-8 sampling (63.0%), and iterative improvement (77.0%). The same planner also improves GPT-5.4 mini and GLM~5.1 from 45.0% and 58.5% to 60.0% and 71.0%. These results demonstrate that learning high-level strategies is an effective and transferable mechanism for improving repository-scale SE agents.

</details>


### [73] [SimWorlds: A Multi-Agent System for Dynamic 3D Scene Creation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01766)
*Chunjiang Liu,Xiaoyuan Wang,Haoyu Chen,Yizhou Zhao,Ming-Hsuan Yang,László A. Jeni*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: SimWorlds 是一个多智能体框架，能够从文本生成动态、可编辑的4D场景（含流体、粒子、刚体、铰接机构等物理效果），通过规划-编码-审查工作流、分层场景协议和运行时状态检查工具来解决时空协调与运动验证难题，并提出了4DBuildBench基准，实验表现优于现有基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM agent系统只能从文本生成静态3D场景，而动态4D场景（含物理仿真：流体流动、粒子发射、刚体碰撞、铰链运动等）虽然在可编辑内容和视频生成/具身AI训练数据方面具有重要价值，却几乎未被探索。主要面临两大挑战：(1) agent需同时协调空间布局、多物理求解器、时序编排、相机与光照；(2) 从渲染视频验证运动正确性远比判断单张图像困难。

Method: 提出SimWorlds多智能体框架：(1) 内置Blender特定程序化知识；(2) 采用planner-coder-reviewer工作流驱动固定顺序的构建阶段；(3) 分层场景协议（layered scene protocol），由确定性验证器强制执行；(4) 运行时状态检查工具套件，可捕获渲染图像无法揭示的机构故障。同时提出4DBuildBench基准，用于评估生成场景的视觉保真度和物理一致性。

Result: 在4DBuildBench基准上的实验表明，SimWorlds在视觉保真度和物理一致性方面均优于现有的动态Blender生成基线方法。

Conclusion: SimWorlds验证了通过多智能体协作与专门的验证/检查机制，能够有效从文本生成物理上合理的动态4D场景，填补了文本到动态场景生成领域的空白，为可编辑内容创作和具身AI训练数据生成提供了新途径。

Abstract: LLM agents are increasingly used to translate natural language into 3D scenes in a procedural way, but existing systems focus on static output. Dynamic 4D scenes from text alone, in which liquids flow, particles emit, rigid bodies cascade, and articulated mechanisms move, remain largely unexplored despite their value as editable content and as physics-grounded training data for video generation and embodied AI. Two challenges set the dynamic case apart from static text-to-scene work: an agent must jointly coordinate spatial layout, multiple physics solvers, temporal sequencing, camera, and lighting in a single coherent scene, and verifying motion correctness from rendered video is fundamentally harder than judging a single image. We present SimWorlds: a multi-agent framework that produces dynamic, editable 4D scenes from text, with Blender-specific procedural knowledge, a planner-coder-reviewer workflow driving a fixed ordered sequence of construction stages, a layered scene protocol enforced by a deterministic verifier, and a runtime-state inspection tool suite that catches mechanism failures the rendered image cannot reveal. We also introduce 4DBuildBench, a benchmark for assessing both visual fidelity and physical consistency of the procedural dynamic 3D scenes generated from text prompts. Experiments show that SimWorlds outperforms prior dynamic Blender generation baselines.

</details>


### [74] [Repair the Amplifier, Not the Symptom: Stable World-Model Correction for Agent Rollouts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01767)
*Xinyuan Song,Zekun Cai*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该论文研究大规模智能体规划图失败后的修复问题，提出WM-SAR（世界模型子图放大修复）方法，通过逆向识别因果子图而非扫描症状，在有限token预算下显著优于传统的工程化修复策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着智能体规划从短工具链扩展到包含数千乃至数万步的持久工作流，失败会发生在大型规划图内部而非孤立预测中。每次失败后重新规划整张图在计算上不现实：全图重放消耗大量上下文预算、使LLM暴露于无关症状、并可能降低长上下文检索质量。现有系统缺乏在保持规划图结构的前提下进行原地修复的"世界模型修正器"（world-model corrector）。

Method: 论文比较了两类修正器：(1) 工程化方法：扫描节点和边，定位可疑局部区域，交由LLM修复；(2) 提出的WM-SAR方法：不从可见症状出发扫描，而是从子图放大（subgraph amplification）逆向工作，识别持续放大错误的节点和边，仅将因果子图发送给LLM进行修复。

Result: 在图仿真和LLM修复实验中，WM-SAR在现实token预算下显著优于工程化修正器，通过紧凑区域实现接近全图的稳定化，并为LLM提供了更清晰的修复目标。

Conclusion: 大规模持久化智能体系统中，针对规划图失败的高效修复不应依赖全图重放或盲目扫描，而应通过因果诊断定位错误源，以最小的子图实现有效修复，WM-SAR正是这一方向的可行方案。

Abstract: As agent planning moves from short tool chains toward persistent workflows with thousands or tens of thousands of steps, failures will occur inside large planning graphs rather than in isolated predictions. Replanning the entire graph after every mistake is neither computationally realistic nor desirable: full-graph replay consumes large context budgets, exposes the LLM to many irrelevant symptoms, and can degrade long-context retrieval. This paper studies the missing component in such systems: a world-model corrector that repairs the failed planning graph in place. We compare two families of correctors. The first is the common engineering approach: scan nodes and edges, choose a suspicious local region, and ask an LLM to repair it. We implement strong engineering LLM correctors and find that they can help, especially when given very large contexts. The second family is our approach, WM-SAR (World-Model Subgraph Amplification Repair): instead of scanning for visible symptoms, it works backward from subgraph amplification, identifies the nodes and edges that keep re-amplifying error, and sends only that causal subgraph to the LLM. Across graph simulations and LLM repair experiments, WM-SAR substantially outperforms engineering correctors under realistic token budgets, achieves near-whole-graph stabilization with a compact region, and gives the LLM a cleaner repair target.

</details>

*Yujin Yang,Heejung Lee*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出一个检索增强的小语言模型框架，以形式概念分析（FCA）作为符号验证回路进行知识扩展，用于本体构建。该框架以种子属性为起点，通过FCA在增长的形式背景上提出蕴含，由检索增强的SLM神谕验证或反例，在罕见共济失调数据集上取得了一定的关系F1和蕴含F1。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本体构建中需决定哪些对象、属性和结构关系应被接受为有效知识。语言模型可从文本中提议此类结构，但其输出可能缺乏支撑或不一致。需要一种将符号推理与语言模型结合的机制，以提供可检验、可验证的知识扩展过程。

Method: 提出一种检索增强小语言模型（SLM）框架，以形式概念分析（FCA）作为符号验证回路。流程如下：(1) 从种子属性出发，FCA在逐步增长的形式背景上生成属性蕴含；(2) 由检索增强的SLM神谕对每条蕴含进行验证，或返回反例；(3) 该神谕还支持隶属判断、一致性检查和属性提议，使得被接受的蕴含、反例、矛盾及修正均可审查。

Conclusion: 检索增强的SLM结合FCA符号验证回路可有效支持本体构建中的知识扩展，提供透明、可审查的推理过程。但蕴含评估严格，少量关系错误即可影响多项蕴含判断，且正样本对象-属性对的识别仍是难点。

Abstract: Ontology construction requires deciding which objects, attributes, and structural relations should be accepted as valid knowledge. Language models can propose such structures from text, but their outputs can still be unsupported or inconsistent. This paper proposes a retrieval-augmented small language model (SLM) framework that uses formal concept analysis (FCA) as a symbolic verification loop for knowledge expansion. Starting from seed attributes, FCA proposes implications over a growing formal context. A retrieval-grounded SLM oracle then validates each implication or returns a counterexample. The oracle also supports incidence judgments, consistency checks, and attribute proposals, making accepted implications, counterexamples, contradictions, and corrections inspectable. In a rare ataxia setting constructed from Orphadata resources, retrieval-grounded 10-seed runs obtain relation F1 of 0.29-0.52 and closure-based implication F1 of 0.22-0.30. Larger seed sets increase the number of evaluated implications and often improve implication F1. The lower implication scores reflect a stricter evaluation of derived implications, where one missed or extra relation can affect several implication judgments. Ablations show that incidence judgments in a fixed object-attribute setting can improve closure-based implication scores. However, identifying positive object-attribute pairs remains difficult even when the candidate objects and attributes are fixed.

Method: 1) 使用线性探针(probes)跨层从残差流激活中解码时间步信息；2) 沿推断时间步相关的低维子空间对模型进行激活引导(steering)；3) 分析该表征在激活空间中的几何结构。
